> Bin directory: /usr/local/bin
> Platform:      unknown-linux-musl

> Tarball URL: https://github.com/starship/starship/releases/latest/download/starship-x86_64-unknown-linux-musl.tar.gz
> Installing Starship, please wait…
✓ Starship latest installed

> Please follow the steps for your shell to complete the installation:
  bash
  Add the following to the end of ~/.bashrc:

	eval "$(starship init bash)"

  zsh
  Add the following to the end of ~/.zshrc:

	eval "$(starship init zsh)"

  ion
  Add the following to the end of ~/.config/ion/initrc:

	eval $(starship init ion)

  tcsh
  Add the following to the end of ~/.tcshrc:

	eval `starship init tcsh`

  xonsh
  Add the following to the end of ~/.xonshrc:

	execx($(starship init xonsh))

  fish
  Add the following to the end of ~/.config/fish/config.fish:

	starship init fish | source

  elvish
  Warning Only elvish v0.17 or higher is supported.
  And add the following to the end of ~/.config/elvish/rc.elv:

	eval (starship init elvish)

  nushell
  Warning This will change in the future.
  Only Nushell v0.96 or higher is supported.
  And add the following to the end of your nu config file (find it by running $nu.config-path in Nushell):

	mkdir ($nu.data-dir | path join "vendor/autoload")
        starship init nu | save -f ($nu.data-dir | path join "vendor/autoload/starship.nu")

  PowerShell
  Add the following to the end of Microsoft.PowerShell_profile.ps1:
  You can check the location of this file by querying the $PROFILE variable in PowerShell.
  Typically the path is ~\Documents\PowerShell\Microsoft.PowerShell_profile.ps1 or ~/.config/powershell/Microsoft.PowerShell_profile.ps1 on -Nix.

	Invoke-Expression (&starship init powershell)

  Cmd
  You need to use Clink (v1.2.30+) with Cmd. Add the following to a file starship.lua and place this file in Clink scripts directory:

	load(io.popen('starship init cmd'):read("*a"))()

[GPG Setup] No GPG key found for hostname: 557db0a3aba1

To generate a GPG key for this machine, run:

  gpg --quick-gen-key "poeaudits (557db0a3aba1) <poeaudits@gmail.com>" ed25519 sign 0

This will:
  - Create an ed25519 signing key (modern, secure, fast)
  - Include the hostname in the key identifier for easy identification
  - Set no expiration (use '1y' instead of '0' for 1-year expiry)

After generating the key, run 'chezmoi apply' again to export the public key.

Alternative: For a key with encryption capability, use:

  gpg --full-gen-key

And enter: poeaudits (557db0a3aba1) <poeaudits@gmail.com>

  Configuration
> Bin directory: /usr/local/bin
> Platform:      unknown-linux-musl
> Arch:          x86_64

> Tarball URL: https://github.com/starship/starship/releases/latest/download/starship-x86_64-unknown-linux-musl.tar.gz
> Installing Starship, please wait…
✓ Starship latest installed

> Please follow the steps for your shell to complete the installation:
  bash
  Add the following to the end of ~/.bashrc:

	eval "$(starship init bash)"

  zsh
  Add the following to the end of ~/.zshrc:

	eval "$(starship init zsh)"

  ion
  Add the following to the end of ~/.config/ion/initrc:

	eval $(starship init ion)

  tcsh
  Add the following to the end of ~/.tcshrc:

	eval `starship init tcsh`

  xonsh
  Add the following to the end of ~/.xonshrc:

	execx($(starship init xonsh))

  fish
  Add the following to the end of ~/.config/fish/config.fish:

	starship init fish | source

  elvish
  Warning Only elvish v0.17 or higher is supported.
  And add the following to the end of ~/.config/elvish/rc.elv:

	eval (starship init elvish)

  nushell
  Warning This will change in the future.
  Only Nushell v0.96 or higher is supported.
  And add the following to the end of your nu config file (find it by running $nu.config-path in Nushell):

	mkdir ($nu.data-dir | path join "vendor/autoload")
        starship init nu | save -f ($nu.data-dir | path join "vendor/autoload/starship.nu")

  PowerShell
  Add the following to the end of Microsoft.PowerShell_profile.ps1:
  You can check the location of this file by querying the $PROFILE variable in PowerShell.
  Typically the path is ~\Documents\PowerShell\Microsoft.PowerShell_profile.ps1 or ~/.config/powershell/Microsoft.PowerShell_profile.ps1 on -Nix.

	Invoke-Expression (&starship init powershell)

  Cmd
  You need to use Clink (v1.2.30+) with Cmd. Add the following to a file starship.lua and place this file in Clink scripts directory:

	load(io.popen('starship init cmd'):read("*a"))()

[GPG Setup] Checking GPG key setup for: 66ad62232e2c
[GPG Setup] No GPG key found for hostname: 66ad62232e2c

To generate a GPG key for this machine, run:

  gpg --quick-gen-key "poeaudits (66ad62232e2c) <poeaudits@gmail.com>" ed25519 sign 0

This will:
  - Create an ed25519 signing key (modern, secure, fast)
  - Include the hostname in the key identifier for easy identification
  - Set no expiration (use '1y' instead of '0' for 1-year expiry)

After generating the key, run 'chezmoi apply' again to export the public key.

Alternative: For a key with encryption capability, use:

  gpg --full-gen-key

And enter: poeaudits (66ad62232e2c) <poeaudits@gmail.com>
